Essays

Women of the South Sea Islands Do Not Kill Chickens 190

— Zhan Lu

| Second Song of Strange Customs of the World |

Cock-a-doodle-doo! Cock-a-doodle-doo! Women of the South Sea Islands are forbidden from killing chickens! Killing chickens is the husband's job, how can you blame a wife? It is the duty of men to wield the knife, it is not proper for women to cut meat; this custom has been passed down for who knows how long? Overseas is strange, strange and stranger! It's not that women don't have the strength to tie up a chicken, it's not that women can't cut a chicken without drawing blood; it's just that there are many taboos involved, and men exclusively master the secrets of killing chickens. When a man wields the knife to kill a chicken, the taste is better than a grand feast; the meat is surely better than bear's paw, the soup is just like drinking nectar. It can be enjoyed by guests in large bites, and the soup can satisfy the wife. If a woman wields the knife, the chicken will not be delicious or flavorful; the meat will be tasteless like chewing wax, and the soup will be as bland as tap water; try tasting it, and you will frown, such bland soup is shameful. Hearing this is laughable, the superstition is full of doubts; but after careful consideration, this custom passed down is also reasonable, women have always been soft-hearted, and do not like slaughtering living things; they don't like it, and their intention is clever; they encourage men to be cruel. They falsely claim that men have a knack for cutting meat, and the men are pleased; they boast that their skills are superior to women, not knowing that they have been tricked! "Note" If I wanted to kill chickens, I would wield the knife. Alas! Not wielding the knife is a woman's virtue, killing chickens is exclusively the job of men; the man kills the chicken and the woman eats it, and the taste is truly unparalleled!

"Note" To put on the charcoal basket is to put on a high hat, borrowing a common saying from our country.

Liang, the God of Wealth, Whose Influence Still Lingers 191

— Yong Zi

| Anesthetizing the People of Nanjing |

This time, I went to Nanjing on official business, and I took care of official matters in one breath, putting public affairs before private interests. After completing the official business, I then indulged myself (not misappropriating public funds) and toured the Qinhuai River, Xuanwu Lake, and Confucius Temple.

The Shandong hollow rich man, Liang the Millionaire, had already disappeared from my mind, but strangely, when I returned from Nanjing, I was filled with Liang, the God of Wealth.

Here's how it happened. The first night I arrived in Nanjing, I stayed in a small inn in Xiaguan, when I overheard a visitor calling on someone in the next room, a fellow provincial from Jiangxi. The two engaged in a heated debate, and finally, the guest indignantly said, "You talk a good game, but you don't pay your debts. You're just like Liang, the God of Wealth from Shandong." With that, he slammed the door and left.

The next day, I was eager to use the pit and liberate myself, so I stepped into the toilet, only to find it teeming with business. I thought, the toilet is a place for wonderful writing, so I might as well take this opportunity to admire the capital's toilet walls. Great, among slogans like "Selling Severe Colds" and "XX Was Here," I found the slogan "Liang, the God of Wealth is here, nothing is taboo." Liang, the God of Wealth, had actually usurped the position of Jiang Taigong.

In the evening, I went to the bathhouse to wash, and the back scrubber scrubbed my back while saying, "Liang, the God of Wealth used to come here to bathe, and I scrubbed his back." He seemed to think that with Liang, the God of Wealth's arrival, even the bathhouse had become a scenic spot, and scrubbing Liang, the God of Wealth's back made one a person of importance. But it is said that Liang, the God of Wealth, never bathed all year round. Whether the back scrubber was lying, I could not verify. According to my friends, the phrase "I am Liang, the God of Wealth" is surprisingly effective for driving away beggars. There are many people in Nanjing who don't know that Japan has already formed a puppet government in the Northeast, but when it comes to Liang, the God of Wealth, no one doesn't know Liang, the God of Wealth's birthday. Therefore, if a great writer were to pick up a pen and write a history of Nanjing, Liang, the God of Wealth, would not be without a place.

Enjoying Snow 192

— Shi Bing

| The Heart Is Cold Enough Without Enjoying the Snow |

It snowed all day the day before yesterday. Sitting at home, I felt even colder because I didn't have a heater. It's better to run outside, so I put on two shoes and went to the road to enjoy the snow. This is also a special way to enjoy the snow!

As soon as I walked out of the alley, I saw three men in suits, their heads shrunk into their coats, talking about dancing. One with a taller body had a particularly wonderful theory. He said, "This smooth and firm snow ground is truly a very good and natural dance floor."

At the tram stop, I met seven or eight female students who had just finished class, wearing fur coats and still complaining about the cold, but they were making plans to go to Zhaofeng Park tomorrow to make a big snowman. One female student was pessimistically saying, "I'm afraid it won't snow again tomorrow, or it will melt, wouldn't that be terrible?"

I think it's best to invite this dance-loving friend, if they have the courage, to go to the Shanhaiguan area, not only can they often dance on the natural smooth floor, but they can also ice skate without spending a penny.

As for these female students who want to build a big snowman, I would like to invite them to visit Guanwai. The snow there is both high and thick, and it will never melt. Moreover, the volunteers there are covered in snow, aren't they a big and lively snowman?

Without enjoying the snow, the heart is cold enough.

Record of the Saraca Flower Pavilion 193

— Yin Qiu

There are two painters in Suzhou: one is Wu Hufan, and the other is Wu Zishen. They are of similar age, share the same ambitions, and appreciate each other's talents and skills. Hufan specializes in cursive and regular script calligraphy. They haven't seen each other for twenty years. Zishen is currently involved in artistic education during turbulent times. His younger brother, Bingyi, who resembles an orchid, is also famous for his paintings, and it seems he is the youngest. His works are pure, fresh, and dashing, just like him. He particularly enjoys traveling far, admiring the grandeur of the Forbidden City and the perilousness of the Great Wall in the north, and the vastness and depth of the Yellow River. Recently, he ascended Mount Tai to watch the sunrise. Wherever he went, he would hold a brush and ink to record the scenic spots, creating travelogues of tens of thousands of words. His spirit grew stronger, and his paintings also improved. After returning, he planted a Saraca tree in his new residence in Baihua Lane. Its flowers are ancient, elegant, and lovely. Mr. Taiyan then inscribed the name of his studio as "Saraca Flower Pavilion." Silan invited about a dozen fellow painters to paint and write within it, forming the Saraca Painting Society. The society gathers twice a month to create paintings together, providing for their shared interests. The proceeds from the paintings are entirely used to help the poor, embodying charity in art, with the noblest of intentions. Silan particularly advocates that art must deeply penetrate the common people to arouse aesthetic awareness and inspire ancient sentiments, which would benefit public morals and customs. He also rented several houses by the North Cang Bridge in Guanqian, establishing another studio, still named Saraca, with bright windows and white walls, elegantly structured, displaying many famous calligraphy and paintings. A corner of the small building has tea bowls and chessboards for resting. It serves as a place for circulating calligraphy and paintings and a gathering place for literati. He also provides Hui ink, Huzhou brushes, She inkstones, Hangzhou paper, as well as ink pads and seals, fulfilling all the needs for painting and writing. On the opening day, I went with Shou Juan. Silan warmly welcomed us, as if we were old friends. Both love flowers with the same passion. Shou Juan loves violets just as Silan loves Saraca flowers. Since living in Suzhou, I have visited his residence twice, where violets bloomed in the courtyard like embroidery. Old Qin Nan painted a "Violet Hermitage" picture and wrote an inscription to display it. Now, Silan's Saraca Flower Pavilion is very close by, shining brightly in the art world. Isn't this a wonderful story of our time? I am happy to record it.

Novel

A Guilty Conscience 195

— Liao Hongshou Juan

When Xiao Man said these words, she seemed less like a mature young woman and more like a charming girl. Sometimes, when she was happy, she would add a few more words: "Little darlings, be good! Listen to me, just focus on keeping your bodies plump and white. Don't let your old ailments return during the seasonal changes. That's how you'll repay us..." All these words, though delivered in a jesting tone, were enough to make his face flush. However, upon careful consideration, every word was affectionate, and every sentence was sincere, naturally increasing his gratitude towards them. The extreme gratitude, in turn, caused him to feel intense sorrow. What he grieved was why he didn't have such a wonderful home. Sometimes, it would even give rise to a strange fantasy. What he imagined was that his body could somehow shrink and become smaller, and then he could throw himself into their loving embrace.

Time quietly slipped away as people busied themselves. In the blink of an eye, spring gracefully descended upon the earth. Among all things in the world, none are more beautiful than the spring countryside. Every blade of grass and every tree basks in the spring light, shedding yesterday's desolation and releasing a vibrant vitality. The air seems to be filled with intoxicating warmth. Everything around is replete with colors. Even the most skilled painter, with his masterful control of colors, could not create such a complete palette. Above, the sky is blue and clear; the clouds are white as fresh cotton; scattered among the fields are菜花 and grass, interspersed with碎金 and翡翠. The swaying weeping willows are as green as mist. Several peach trees, swaying in the wind, reveal the blushing cheeks of young girls. People with sensitive natures, when faced with such a scene, how could they not be intoxicated? Not only humans, but even the birds are unwilling to let this spring pass by lightly. They also call their companions, flying and dancing on the newly adorned branches, singing romantic ditties that require no effort to compose. The butterflies, not skilled at singing, take advantage of this fragrant season to freely wear the charming new clothes bestowed upon them by nature, busy visiting their lovers—the wildflowers that stand alone and appreciate their own beauty by the roadside. This is probably when God, drunk on fine wine, suddenly became excited and inspired by an aesthetic thought, and thus used his greatest artistic skills to adorn so many pleasing sounds and colors, both to amuse himself and to delight mankind.

He deeply remembered that, at this time, the invisible spring invitations often invited him and the Dongfang Sheng couple to this quiet and beautiful road. Sometimes, the three of them went out together; sometimes, Xiao Man was unable to spare the time due to household chores, so he and Dongfang Sheng went together; there were also times when Dongfang Sheng had no interest in going out, so he was accompanied by the childlike Xiao Man, a pair like children, jumping here.

Shanghai Night Talk 196

— Zhang Ruo Yu

(Two) Black Eyes

Ten years ago, after reading French writer Alphonse Daudet's "Little Thing," the heroine with the big black eyes in that novel has remained in my memory to this day.

Black eyes are a special treasure endowed to Eastern girls. How can fair-haired lads enjoy碧綠蔚藍秋波? They always harbor vague yearnings and mysterious notions about black eyes.

Near Avenue Joffre and Avenue du Roi Albert, in a narrow lane, there is a mysterious midnight dance hall. The dance hall is a茅屋-style hall, with walls painted with vividly colored patterns: bright red, bright green, deep yellow, deep blue, with thick lines, expressing the flavor of primitive tribal art. The walls are covered with尖角 shape, colorful felt carpets, even more luxurious and刺戟 than Persian Tianjin specialties, adding a layer of warmth and charm to the whole room.

The entrance is a corridor with frescoes of strange figures. A White Russian old man, wearing a royal uniform and adorned with medals and寶星 on his chest, is managing the cloakroom.

Walking into the grand dance floor is like being in an Arabian palace. Turkish music and American red-skinned Indian jazz震蕩 women's hearts and agitate men's desires. And those百色 female dance partners wearing five-colored scarves and red包頭 silk, their black eyes wide open, their tired, long eyelashes drooping, those pairs of big, round black eyes逼視 you,挑逗 you; if you are a膽小的 man, can't stand such charm挑逗? You will surely feel cramped, even your face will blush.

Raising your head, on the back wall of the music stage, are a pair of black eyes. The crazed dancing men and women of all countries and styles dare not look directly at this pair of powerful, mysterious eyes, and in his and her eyes, they see the opponent's fire-like green and blue eyes.

The sky is always a vast blue, a large piece of blue陰丹士林 fabric covering the simple roof. There, you can't see white walls, nor even half a piece of gray tile.

After twelve o'clock, at the moment of handover between last night and this morning, the dance floor begins to liven up. People coming out of the last show in the cinema, or those who have finished the last dance in another dance hall, flow here like tides.

A night traveler on Avenue Joffre is a regular at this midnight dance hall. He praises its advantages: there is no class, no gentility, no nationality, no distinction between races. Mr. Black can dance with Mrs. White. The waiter can sit down and share a cigarette with you in his spare time, or talk about family matters and entertainment. You don't have to worry. If you are hot, you can take off your jacket, even turn up the sleeves of your shirt. Even if you are a little drunk, you won't slip and fall while dancing on the floor. However, there is heat, there is charm, there is the逼視 of the black eyes on the wall, and there is the挑逗 of the black eyes in the hall.

This unique mysterious midnight dance hall on Avenue Joffre is called "Black Eyes."

All those who remember the heroine in "Little Thing" might as well go to this dance hall and spend a night through the wee hours; you can find black eyes among black eyes.

Commercial News

The Calm Gold Market Without Financial Ripples

Rose 5.6 Taels and Broke Through 800 Taels 197

According to yesterday's foreign telegraphs, London大條 (gold bars) rose slightly both in the near and distant futures at .0625. Both the British-American and American-British exchange rates also saw slight increases. The Bank of America also rose by .125. Although the silver market for forward contracts saw only small gains according to private telegrams from banks, market sentiment was excellent. Although it opened at a flat rate of 797.3 taels, this price was completely unexpected. Therefore, it rose immediately after opening to 801.7 taels. At this time, the bank's opening price was also better than the previous closing. Although the domestic market could not be called tight, it was very stable. Therefore, the gold price was able to stand above 800 taels. The HSBC exchange rate also narrowed, allowing the gold market to have an opportunity to rise. The result was a closing price of 802.9 taels. There were very few large transactions throughout the day, and market sentiment was very stable. Difficulties in Concluding Rural Economic Downturn's Outstanding Debts 210

The difficulties in concluding the current outstanding debts have been detailed in this newspaper. According to reports from the silver and money industry, the collection of outstanding debts from foreign ports is even more urgent than last year. For example, the outstanding debts from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, in the year 21, frequently encountered national disasters and commercial decline reached its peak. The harvest failures of agricultural products are undeniable, and the economic distress cannot be salvaged by human power. Those who had no choice but to request轉賬 (transfer) were common, but the Shanghai financial community, for the sake of審慎 (caution) and self-defense, was unwilling to reluctantly agree. It is necessary to make a serious further collection effort, but no matter how strictly it is urged, what is received is still寥寥 (very little).

Five to Six Hundred Boxes Loaded on Yangtze River Liners Daily 220

With the spring sales season starting for inland silk weaving factories, there is a high demand for rayon. Rayon, previously bought on a futures basis last month by the Yangtze River dealers, is now being shipped in batches.

In recent days, Yangtze River liners such as the Jianguo have been loading large quantities of rayon destined for various Yangtze River ports, totaling five to six hundred boxes. It is said that goods purchased by Sichuan dealers are being transshipped from Hankou to Sichuan.

Grains

Early Rice and Yang Du Xian Arriving in the City, Prices Firm 221

Thin rice in the Southern Market and Yin Yuan Sales are Dull, Falling 20-30 Cents

(North Shanghai): Yesterday, over ten shipments arrived in Hexia. Transactions for high-quality white japonica rice were average, while mid- to lower-quality rice sold reasonably well. The market for high-quality rice was stable, while mid- to lower-quality rice was tight, exceeding market expectations. Arrivals of thin rice were sluggish, with prices weakening. Arrivals of early rice were limited but sales were active, with prices showing a tightening trend. Arrivals of Yang Du sharp rice were not strong, but sales were good, with prices tightening, exceeding market expectations. Arrivals of port-specific sharp rice were lacking. Arrivals of Yin Bai Yuan were not numerous, and retail sales were quite good, with prices increasing by 10-20 cents.

(South Shanghai): Yesterday, there were 30-40 arrivals. The market condition is that the approaching end of the lunar year has led to retail congestion, and bulk buyers have stopped purchasing. Therefore, rice from Changzhou, Suzhou, and Nantong, including thin rice, has fallen by 20-30 cents. Arrivals of Yin Yuan were numerous, but sales were sluggish, also falling by about 30 cents. There was no market for Du Yang sharp rice.

Guest Xian and Minhua Rice Remain Active

Foreign Merchants Selling Futures for Foreign Rice 222

Yesterday's Guest Xian market saw continued inquiries from Fuzhou dealers. Arrivals were not numerous, and remaining stocks were mainly held by囤户(tun hu) (speculators). Floating stocks were scarce, resulting in a gradual increase in market prices. A total of 579 bags of Hunan processed rice were handled by Fuzhou dealers, priced from $9.22 to $9.15.

Although foreign rice stocks are sufficient, floating stocks on the market have already been sold off. Most of the current stock is held by foreign merchants and a small number of囤户(tun hu) (speculators), who are unwilling to sell due to high costs. However, Annam rice prices are showing a downward trend. Yesterday, foreign merchants were again soliciting new trades. Saigon No. 1 rice was only 4 liang and 2-3 qian, and small-grain rice was only 3 liang and 7-8 qian. Saigon rice was under $9, and small-grain rice was under $8. The local market price was about 70-80 cents higher. However, orders are placed for the long term. Although rice merchants are tentatively buying, they are wary due to past experiences and dare not rashly complete the transaction.

Flour Market Initially Weak, Then Strong 223

Yesterday's flour market showed an initial weakness followed by a strengthening trend in all months after the opening in the morning and afternoon. As the price of foreign wheat continued to fall slightly by 20 cents, sentiment weakened at the initial opening in the morning. The current month fell to a low of $1.29425, and distant months also fell by about 500. However, after the second session, the market across all months gradually recovered. Although customer demand appeared quiet, Fuzhou and other new buyers were experiencing a shortage of現貧軋缺 (xian pin ya que), and there was some resistance to decline for January and February, stabilizing market sentiment. By the afternoon opening, trading across all months had not improved, but factories continued to resist declining prices for January and February. Customer demand also saw some trading in distant months, leading to a gradual increase in opening prices. Despite the frequent deliveries of foreign wheat, the current shortage of spot goods makes it difficult for market sentiment to decline. (Fu Feng increased by 8 cents, and Xin Tai increased by 6 cents.) As a result, the current month rose by 1 cent compared to the previous day, February rose by 2 cents, March rose by 1.25 cents, April rose by 1.5 cents, May rose by 1.25 cents, and June rose by 1.75 cents.

Wheat Market Still Lacks Momentum 224

(Impact of Arriving Foreign Wheat Prepared for Delivery)

Yesterday's futures wheat market showed an initial weakness followed by stability across all months after the opening in the morning and afternoon. In the morning, as foreign wheat prices continued to fall by over 20 cents, sentiment softened, and opening prices across all months fell by 1-2 cents compared to the previous day. By the afternoon opening, the current month was approaching delivery, and although buyers wanted to resist the decline, sellers were experiencing fatigue due to the arrival of foreign wheat prepared for delivery. Distant months initially remained weak, but later improved as the flour market turned better, leading to improved sentiment. However, traders still hold several hundred cars of goods that have not been hedged, so there will be further movement after the goods arrive. As a result, the current month fell by 2 cents compared to the previous day, February and March fell by 1 cent, and April remained unchanged. (16th) Chicago wheat initially rose due to purchases from the East, but later fell due to the influence of 玉蜀 (yu shu) (corn) and profit-taking by bullish investors. A total of 20 million bushels were traded on the 14th. The market prices for the 16th are listed below:

Closing Price Compared to Previous Day

May Futures 46.875 down 0.875

July Futures 47.000 down 0.500

September Futures 47.875 down 0.25

Soybean Market Increases, Then Slumps 225

The high-quality soybean market is stable, and sales continue to be good. Market conditions have been stable recently, with consistent increases and decreases. The market appears to be preparing for a new year rally. Yesterday, three cars of Southern Suzhou soybeans were traded, all for immediate delivery. Three cars of Dingjia State and Zhengyangguan soybeans were purchased by inland oil mills. Two hundred bags of Chongming Sand soybeans were sold off and purchased by local dealers. Two hundred and seventy bags of Xuzhou white beans were traded at steady prices. One hundred bags of raw peanuts were sold, with prices increasing and then slumping. The oil market continued to rise, but the gains were not strong, only fluctuating by a small amount. A London dispatch from the 16th reported that soybean oil was unchanged, soybeans were priced at 7 pounds per ton, and rapeseed oil was priced at 29.0 per 120 pounds.

Sugar Market

Chaoqing Continues to Arrive, Over a Thousand Bags 226

Offer Prices Show No Sign of Loosening

Yesterday's sugar market had good sentiment at the initial opening due to firmer標金 (biao jin) (benchmark prices), but failed to rise further due to limited purchases. The Guild set the price for No. 24 coarse white sugar at 15.8 taels, but there were few takers. It was later traded at 15.75 taels per 100 bags. The price for No. 20 medium white sugar was slightly lower, set at 15.325 taels. A Jian dealer continued to offer 100 bags of 刁靑 (diao qing) (high-quality sugar) at 9.5 taels. According to the letter, the cost of Chaoqing, which arrived from Shantou on the Taikoo ship Suiyang, is above 9 taels. It is said that dealers are unwilling to loosen prices further before the end of the settlement period.

According to New York telegrams, spot prices fell slightly by 0.03125 to 7.1875 cents. Futures for March fell slightly by 3 points to 6.5 cents, December fell slightly by 1 point to 8.3 cents, and the remaining months fell slightly by 2 points. January was at 6.7 cents, May at 7 cents, July at 7.4 cents, and September at 7.8 cents. London sugar futures fell by 1 penny to 4.225 for March, fell by 1.25 pennies to 5.50 for May, and fell by 1.25 pennies to 5.350 for August (per 120 pounds). Java white sugar was unchanged at 7 shillings and 9 pence.

Metals

Overseas Prices Rising 227

Tianjin and Qingdao Merchants Returning North

Metal trading is very slow because of the closure of the lunar year and the winding up of accounts by customer groups and factories. Many of the Tianjin, Qingdao, and other groups are returning north because of port closures and rampant rumours in their local areas, further depopulating the market. Prices are virtually unchanged because of minuscule levels of imports and exports, but news that overseas prices have risen continuously for several days is helping stabilize market sentiment and generate price optimism. Items such as tinplate, plain iron, galvanized iron, and corrugated iron all show a bullish trend.

Overseas telegrams from London and New York report that the price of first-grade tinplate has risen by 0.1125. There is still no available tin, as there are very few transactions in first-grade tinplate. A London telegram from the 16th reports that the prices of copper, tin, and zinc have fallen, while lead has risen slightly, and antimony and tungsten are unchanged. The same day, a New York telegram reports that the price of No. 2 pig iron is $12.5 per ton, No. 24 black iron sheet (per 100 pounds) is $2.05, No. 24 white iron sheet is $1.80, and tinplate is $4.25 per box.

Statistics on China's Tea Exports in the 21st Year Under Dumping of Japanese Tea in India 228

British Market Seized by India and Japan...Russia is Seeking Self-Sufficiency

Africa, Once Exclusively Occupied by Chinese Tea...Japanese Tea Has Made a Head-On Collision

In addition to strictly inspecting for adulteration, coloring, and other malpractices in tea destined for foreign countries, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry also publishes monthly sales figures and export quantities to provide a reference for the tea industry. The full-year report for the 21st year has now been completed. Although this report only refers to direct exports from Shanghai and transshipments from Hankou and other ports, Shanghai and Hankou have now become the two major markets for Chinese tea exports. The figures contained in this report account for more than three-quarters of total exports. The export figures are as follows:

Shanghai Tea Inspection and Export Statistics for the 21st Year of the Republic

Category: Green Tea Red Tea Brick Tea Other Tea Total

Country: Dan Dan Dan Dan Dan

United Kingdom 493.25 28,509.58 515.56

France 15,137.34 3,225.49 55.56

Germany 41.25 2,022.67 6.38

Holland 26.65 1,435.00 19

Spain 281.61 465.28

Turkey, Bolivia, etc. 1,047.30 33.76

United States 30,512.14 17,273.11 1,128.41

Canada 469.42 98.61 15.11

Africa 151,953.49 14,415.88 17.50

Russia 7,777.57 1,141.26 726,798.54

India 16,447.45 5,527.38 79.31

Hong Kong 3,568.15 2,867.12 5.25 5,970.04

Other Countries 492.18 1,507.56 5.76 108.50

Total 228,247.80 76,522.50 226,809.55 7,894.09

According to the total figures in the table above, exports to Russia are the highest, followed by Africa, and then the United States and the United Kingdom. Most of the Russian figures are brick tea, while the combined amount of green tea and black tea, which used to be important, is now less than 10,000 dan. This is due to the leading sales of Indian black tea and Japanese green tea, as well as Russia's self-cultivation of tea in recent years. (Chinese black tea exports to Russia reached a maximum of 400,000 dan, and green tea was about 150,000 dan). The United Kingdom has historically been the largest market for Chinese tea exports, with black tea reaching a maximum of 1 million dan, and green tea being less, around 80,000 to 90,000 dan. Last year, the total amount of black and green tea was less than 30,000 dan, a decrease of two-thirds compared to the peak period. Although Africa has seen a slight increase, last year it was also affected by the dumping of Japanese tea. Japanese green tea began to be imported into Africa in 1931, but the quantity at that time was only 15,000 pounds. By the end of November last year, it had jumped to over 500,000 pounds. This year, it will inevitably engage in a head-on collision with Chinese tea. In the past two years, the total number of Chinese tea exports has largely been maintained, but prices have also decreased by about one-third. The future of Chinese tea is truly heartbreaking.

Free Talk

Teacher and Disciple (3) 254

— Xingjuan

After a while, some dowry items were chosen and taken away. I said, this definitely isn't a good person!

A few days later, that young fellow came again. I ignored him, but the master eagerly went to entertain him.

First, he chatted with the master in a familiar, disrespectful way. Then, I saw him lean close to the master's ear, whispering some secret, devilish things!

But the master's smiling face immediately turned serious, and he repeatedly shook his head.

The young fellow seemed very unhappy and left.

The next morning, as the sun rose, the master again carried a string of shovels, chisels,... to the street to sell.

The sun shone into his shop. My junior sister and I were playing with coins. The master didn't return.

The sun shone directly on the center of the street. After Ah Zhen and I ate lunch, the master didn't return.

The sun shone past the house across the street. Ah Zhen and I sat at the door waiting. The master didn't return.

The sun set. Ah Qi, the wonton seller from Gaodun, ran in, panting and covered in sweat! He said our master had stolen a pair of gold bracelets from the Chun Tai-ye family and had been arrested by the officials! The master said Da Mao should manage the shop and Ah Zhen should go quickly, otherwise, he would be killed!

Ah Zhen cried out and ran off with Ah Qi like she was flying. I was like a lost bean, unable to decide what to do, my heart burning like red iron...

The first night, the moon hung in the sky, and I wandered in circles in the moonlight! Alone.

The second night, the moon hung in the sky, and I wandered in circles in the moonlight! Alone.

The third night, the master came back. I asked, "Where's junior sister!" The master ignored me, his eyes fixed on the empty space with anger. The moon hung in the sky, and he wandered in circles in the moonlight. The master shed tears in the moonlight. Two people.

From then on, the master no longer went to the streets to sell. He let the business in our shop decline day by day. He spent all the money he earned each day on baijiu, drinking himself into a drunken stupor, and then tried to beat me with a large hammer. He didn't even think that I had been hungry for days and hadn't had a good meal! I wanted to leave, but I was worried about my junior sister. I dreamed of my junior sister returning every day, but when I woke up, it was all empty! My heart, my body, my whole being was filled with pain!

I thought, junior sister should come back, right? Oh, then I'd be really happy! But day after day, month after month, I never saw her return.

In some dreams, I saw her in that old thief Chun Daye's house, dressed like a courtesan. In other dreams, I saw her being devoured alive by a wolf, so pitiful! I didn't dare to think about it. Whenever I thought about it, tears fell like rain.

Junior sister should come back, right?

These days are truly unbearable! (The End)

Release Peace 255

— Xianju

I remember when the European War ended, a celebration meeting was held in Beijing. Mr. Cai Yuanpei gave a speech, saying in essence that justice had triumphed over might, and from then on, the world could embark on a path of peace. The historical facts at home and abroad over the past ten years have proven that Mr. Cai's "peace" dream at that time was ultimately just a "fantasy" of a flower in a mirror and the moon in the water.

However, now, our country, from the court to the common people, is still dreaming this kind of peaceful fantasy. What exactly is the content of peace? Because the interests of each social stratum are different, there are also different interpretations. Generally speaking, there are roughly three points:

1. The peace of the strong. The tiger said to the sheep, "I am extremely fond of peace. As long as you don't resist, my appetite is limited. After I eat my fill every day, I will naturally shut up. Your remaining lives will also get a considerable amount of peace." This is the kind of peace that imperialists demand from weak nations and warlords demand from oppressed groups.

2. The peace of the weak. The psychology of the weak is a psychology of clinging to life and fearing death. They dare not offer the slightest resistance to the insults and slaughter of aggressors and oppressors, but they are unwilling to openly write the "cross" of surrender. Therefore, they shout peace at the strong. This peace is "shameful servility" kowtowing beneath the enemy's bayonets. It is a shameless peace. Shameless peace and the unreasonable peace of the strong are both the great enemies of true human peace, and we should use all our strength to smash them.

3. True peace is built on the foundation of equality and freedom for all people, not on the foundation of the strong bullying the weak and the rich oppressing the poor. In this kingdom of peace, not only is there political equality and freedom, but there is also economic equality and freedom. The problems of everyone are not forced by the so-called laws and force of a few powerful people on one side, but are adjusted by the conventions of the social labor organization. During the transition period from the existing system to the true kingdom of peace, there is naturally still a need to replace the coercive laws and force of a minority with the coercive laws and force of the majority. But this is a necessary means to get on the road to true peace and naturally cannot be said to be a destruction of peace.

Fireside Chat 256

— Yu Dafu

(1)

Freedom of speech is still out of the question in China. According to the declaration of the China League for Civil Rights, "The civil rights demanded by the Chinese people through revolutionary sacrifices have not yet been realized, which is most distressing. Records of suppressing public opinion and illegal arrests and killings are common in newspapers; even young men and women are sometimes suspected of being political prisoners and are inevitably subjected to secret military trials." Judging from this, the right to personal freedom (Habeas Corpus) given to the people in Europe during the Dark Ages has still not been obtained in China. It was the same when King Li of Zhou and Qin Shi Huang were in power three or four thousand years ago, and it is still the same now, three or four thousand years after the success of the revolution. May I ask, if a person cannot even maintain the safety of their own body, then what is there to say about freedom of speech? People without freedom of speech can exist, but can there be a kind of person without a body in this world?

The British novelist Compton Mackenzie was recently fined two thousand yuan for writing a memoir that leaked secrets from when he served as a British intelligence agent in Greece during the Great War. Fortunately, this happened in England, the cradle of liberalism, so C.M.'s head was saved. If it had happened in China, everyone can imagine what the outcome would have been like? George Bernard Shaw, relying on his age and experience, said that England could abandon India, but only received a warning from the colonial governor. Imagine what the ending would have been like if this had happened in China.

Therefore, I feel that in today's China, advocating and striving for freedom of speech is still a luxury for those who advocate it.

(2)

Mr. Wang Weizi asked for an inscription for a painting of an autumn wind on horseback by Chen Zihe. It has been two or three months since I handed in my assignment. Now, I occasionally flip through my diary and see this matter, so I came up with four crooked poems.

A picture of youthful frustration, with remnant mountains and waters vaguely recognized; the autumn wind on horseback over Xianxia Ridge, carries the boat girl of the nine surnames, no?

Because he was returning from Fujian in frustration at the time, he thought of Bao Zhupo's Jiangshan boat. This story comes from Li Chunke's diary.

On the Various Customs of Celebrating the New Year in My Hometown 257

— Dasheng

It has been snowing heavily for the past few days, creating quite a scene of the end of winter. According to the calendar, today should be the twenty-third day of the twelfth lunar month. Although my footprints have been like duckweed for several years, and the so-called "auspicious occasions" can no longer stir up "poetic feelings" in the heart of a wanderer, I often feel a sense of longing whenever I think of the customs around the New Year in my hometown and the games of the children. "I ask, do the sand and dust of my hometown still cover the footprints of my youth?" Thinking of this often makes me feel desolate!

× × × × ×

My hometown is on the banks of Dongting Lake in Hunan. In my hometown, after today, tomorrow (the twenty-fourth) is called "Little New Year." On the evening of the Little New Year, it is said that the Kitchen God goes to heaven to report the good and evil deeds of this family, so every family must worship the Kitchen God that night and burn a memorial written on yellow paper at the stove, asking him to say a few good words for this family when he reports to the Heavenly Court. However, it is impossible to know whether the Kitchen God accepts this sweet talk and bribery. Probably the Kitchen God has become smarter this year.

After the Little New Year, the New Year is really getting closer and closer. Mothers have to warn their children not to cry and not to talk too much, and they especially forbid the use of unlucky words such as "death," "ghost," and "bad luck." Children are constantly craning their necks, hoping that the New Year will come soon. "Adults look forward to transplanting rice seedlings, and children look forward to celebrating the New Year." These words vividly portray the different mentalities of adults and children, and at the same time describe the sorrow of adults.

The last day of the twelfth month is called New Year's Eve. On New Year's Eve, the whole family has to "stay up all night," and the incense candles in front of the spirits are kept burning all night long. When the rooster crows and the east is about to dawn, the situation becomes more and more tense. Everyone deliberately puts on a happy face and doesn't talk much. They light torches and prepare firecrackers. The whole family prepares to go out. The ritual of going out is to open the door, first the head of the family bows to the vast and boundless heavens and earth, and then they set off the firecrackers with a crackling sound. The longer the firecrackers are set off, the more it shows the wealth of this family. After setting off the firecrackers, they happily go home. Some even carry back a large pile of firewood, which is meant to symbolize "bringing wealth home."

As soon as they enter the door, everyone is busy "wishing each other a happy New Year." Naturally, the younger generation starts by wishing the elders a happy New Year, kowtowing and bowing. If there are many people in this family, then you bow to me, I bow to you, and you have to say "Congratulations, congratulations" in your mouth, making a mess. This is really an extremely interesting drama. After the family has paid their respects, they then pay their respects to the neighbors on the left and right, and then to relatives and friends in distant places. When I was at home, I was most afraid of this routine.

From the first day of the first lunar month to the fifteenth, everyone doesn't work. Some play cards, some play with dragons, play with lanterns, or play with lions. Everyone probably knows about playing with dragons and playing with lions. As for playing with lanterns, it's also similar to the variety shows in Shanghai's Great World. A young man and a young woman sing some lyrics and songs about flirting between men and women. There are also many very good ones, but unfortunately I can't remember them all.

The evening of the fifteenth is called the Lantern Festival, and the children play the game of "Welcoming the Seventh Sister." The Seventh Sister is also called "Lipo," and the children revere her as a goddess, saying that she can divine good and bad fortune. The method of welcoming the Seventh Sister is to wrap a bamboo chopstick and a flower around a bamboo sieve, and then put some rice in a plate and insert one end of the bamboo chopstick into the rice. Two unmarried girls each lift the bamboo sieve with one finger, constantly chanting incantations. When the Seventh Sister comes, the chopstick on the bamboo sieve draws words on the rice, and then the people standing quietly next to them are busy asking about longevity and the year's fortunes. The incantation is the most interesting. "The first month is the first month, all the grass is green. Please Seventh Sister, ask about the year's fortunes. Ask about the year's fortunes, whether it's true or false, ask about the year's fortunes, whether it's false or true. On the fifteenth day of the first month, there are bustling flower lanterns, and the flower lanterns are spinning around. Swing on the tree..."

Unfortunately, I can't remember it completely, I only remember this much.

Long Creative Work

The Crossroads of the Times and Love (Continued Draft) 258

— Zhang Ziping

"What exactly is your relationship with them?"

Hearing Madame Hezi say that she didn't care about them, he couldn't help but cheer up, and his attitude changed, asking her gently, "You can't tell me?"

She had just eaten a piece of bread and answered him shyly. After saying that, she smiled with a blush.

Her attitude aroused another wave of suspicion in his heart. The fire of jealousy is more violent than any kind of flame. Indeed, his face turned green again.

"Is he your old flame from before?"

He asked her in Cantonese, jokingly.

"Oh my, Mr. Lin looks down on people too much! If he were my old flame, would I dare let him come here? He wouldn't let me just sit in your room, would he?"

After she said that, she burst out laughing. Haiquan felt that what she said made sense and couldn't help but blush.

"The weather is nice today, Mr. Lin, how about going for a walk in the suburbs? Pincinc!"

"Let's go in the afternoon."

He couldn't deny the love between them no matter what. And he also felt that he couldn't leave her during this period. Leaving her would mean tasting the bitterness of loneliness. As long as he didn't touch on concrete issues, he would maintain a special friendship with this woman of a different race. He suddenly expressed his compromise again.

"Why not take a day off? Such good weather. Such a beautiful day, how many times do we have that in life? What does a day's work count for?" she said with a smile. He thought, this is clearly a temptation.

"I have an important letter to deliver to the school."

"Why not just mail it with a two-cent stamp?"

"It's an important letter."

This was a letter of recommendation that Zhuo Shuhua had asked him to get from Ren Shushi, recommending her brother to work in the ×× bureau. Last night, he had dinner at Ren's house. Because of this matter, he felt it was very inconvenient to mention it to Ren Jinhua. It was only later that Mrs. Ren and her husband indirectly said it. Haiquan really didn't expect that Ren Shushi would readily agree to his request and specially wrote this letter of recommendation for him. At that time, he really had an unspeakable gratitude. Because he was holding this letter, he could brag to Zhuo Shuhua even more.

"You can register the important letter."

"Then send it by express mail."

Haiquan agreed to accompany her out, first to the post office to send the express mail, and then to the park for a stroll.

"Thank you so much, Mr. Lin!"

She said this time in Japanese, bowing to Haiquan with a smile.

On Treason 259

— Wu

The matter of treason may not seem so high-sounding, but now that we have reached the point where "everyone is selling the country," it is also worthy of discussion.

Originally, treason does not necessarily incur any major penalties, especially when the country is no longer a country and one cannot enjoy the slightest protection from this country, so it is better to sell it off and let everyone taste the true taste of being a slave to a conquered nation. Perhaps this is the ultimate goal of the kind and virtuous descendants of the Yellow Emperor. However, treason is not an easy task, and not every ordinary person can do it, because all the powerful figures are already engaged in wholesale and retail, and we small and petty patriots have no chance to skim any oil. But doesn't this seem unreasonable? We are all people of a ancient country of more than four thousand years, and we have the right to sell our country. How can you few people handle it all? Thinking about it, I feel resentful, so we must fight for this right to sell our country. Moreover, the art of treason also needs to be studied. As for our art of treason, it's not bad either. When we buy and sell inferior goods, we still say "I dare not lag behind others in loving the country." Under the banner of "long-term resistance," we certainly don't need to organize volunteer troops. In order to learn the skills of being slaves to a conquered nation, we might as well have a few sets of "dancing to save the country," "artistic performances to save the country," "art to save the country," and "entertainment to save the country" to make others forget the national crisis. Our doctors, scholars, and celebrities, in order to keep their positions as "ministers of a conquered nation," might as well strongly support the Lytton Report. Our literati and officials, in order to prevent the people from truly expanding the national war and hindering their treasonous business, are vigorously promoting "internal pacification." Our artists, fearing that the country will not be destroyed, keep repeating the old tune of "art for art's sake."

Looking at it this way, it is no longer a question of whether China should be sold off. It's just that everyone is striving to work hard to sell the country, seeing who can achieve great success in it. Only the Northeast Volunteer Army in the frozen land does not understand the benefits of treason and desperately fights the imperialists, and also hopes that the generous philanthropists in Guannei who are enthusiastic about selling the country will provide material assistance. This is truly excellent and outstanding.

Science

How Records are Made 260

— Zhong Sheng

Everyone knows that the phonograph and records were invented by the American inventor Thomas Edison. But Edison's original method was very incomplete. It took a long time of improvement to reach the perfect state it is in now!

At first, the method of making records invented by Edison was called the "horn-style recording method." The method is to place a "sound box" (Sound Box) at the rear end of a metal horn; this sound box has a thin mica film attached to it. Therefore, the music and vocal sounds played outside the horn are collected in the horn tube, directly causing the film to vibrate: the film then transmits its vibration to a steel gauge, and the steel needle engraves the sound waves on the rotating wax plate.

However, this method is very incomplete. First, the vibration frequency of sounds emitted by humans is usually about 26 to 1,700 cycles per second, while the vibration frequency of sounds played by musical instruments is about 30 to 7,000 cycles per second. As for the vibration frequency of sounds that people's ears can hear, it is 30 to 20,000 cycles per second. However, the sound waves that this horn-style recording method can collect are only 300 to 2,500 cycles per second: no matter how good the vibrating membrane is, it can only collect 80 to 4,000 cycles of sound waves. Second, during recording, the sound quality can change due to the horn's reverberation. Third, when recording sound waves, the vibrating membrane and the wax plate will generate resistance, so the recorded sound waves in a certain range will become weaker, and even recorded as being very different from the original sound. Fourth, therefore, the sounds emitted by low-pitched instruments are very difficult to record. In short, records made using the horn-style recording method are not very perfect and cannot be regarded as a reproduction of the original sound. They are just a kind of flat "canned sound" that is more similar to the original sound.

Later, after joint research by the American Victor company and the Western Electric company, in 1924, they completed a kind of "electrical recording method." This method uses a "vacuum tube amplification device," and this method can collect all the sounds that human hearing can sense. As a result, the horn-style recording method became a past "relic of the scientific world!"

This electrical recording method does not use a horn, but instead uses a "microphone" (Microphone). The recording of sound waves must go through the following sequence: (1) microphone (2) amplifier (Amplifier) (3) electrical recording machine (Electric Recorder) (4) wax plate (Wax Plate).

Initially, the sound of the human throat or the music from musical instruments is sensed by the microphone, and the sound waves are transformed into electrical waves: but these electrical waves are very thin and weak and are not enough to vibrate the recording machine, so they must first be transmitted to the amplifier to "amplify" them into electrical waves millions of times stronger: these amplified electrical waves act on the recording machine and are then converted back into the original sound waves, causing the jewel-made recording needle to vibrate, engraving the dense sound waves on the rotating wax plate. The wax plate made in this way is called a "recording wax plate" (Plate Recording Wax Plate).

Next, a mixed coating is applied to the surface of the recording wax plate to make it an electrical conductor, and it is immersed in a copper electrolytic bath, and its surface is electroplated with copper until the plated copper plate is about one thirty-second of an inch thick. Then it is taken out of the bath, and the plated copper plate is separated from the wax plate, so the sound wave recording on the wax plate is copied very accurately onto the copper plate. This is called the "father master" (Original Master).

After the father master is made, another "mother master" must be made using the father master as a model. The method is to first apply a release solution to the surface of the father master, and then immerse it in a nickel (Nickel) electrolytic bath for about an hour, then its surface will be plated with a layer of nickel. Then immerse it in a copper electrolyte solution and plate a layer of copper plate on the back of the nickel surface. Then it is taken out of the electrolytic bath, and the two cast plates are peeled off, then the new cast plate with a nickel surface is the "mother master" (Mother). This mother master can reproduce the original sound on the phonograph just like an ordinary record. Although I have not seen the records of the Chinese recording company, maybe they are the kind of "mother master" items.

After the mother master is made, a release solution is applied to its surface and a thin layer of nickel is plated: then it is placed in a copper electrolytic deep liquid and a copper layer is plated. Then take it out and peel off the two sides, nail a copper plate to the back of the new cast plate, and then cut it into the shape of an ordinary record; this is called the "stamper" (Stanper). What is printed with this stamper is the record we use: so if this stamper has some small marks, a new stamper must be made from the mother master using the above method, otherwise the printed record will not be perfect.

The raw materials for ordinary records are shellac rubber, (Carbo Black), and other filling materials produced in India, the Americas, and the East Indies. These raw materials must first be crushed, heated, and refined into a rectangular block using special crushing machines and mixers. This is called a (Biscuit), and each block is just right for printing a record. This raw material is placed on a steam heating plate to make it soft, and then placed between the original plate A and B, and squeezed and cooled, then it becomes an ordinary record.

But before the records are sold, they must first undergo precise listening tests. The first twenty-five records printed from each type must be completely free of defects before they can pass: otherwise, the stamper has defects, so a new stamper must be cast from the mother master.

Literature and Art

Winter Wind 261

— Wang Zhuyu

Piercing winter wind blows again,

Cotton clothes are light, suffering in the cold;

Do those in fox fur know?

There are frozen corpses of lone soldiers in the north!

Rainy Morning 262

— Wang Congxin

The continuous drizzle washes the dust into the empty air,

Fresh from a sweet dream, I rush to work;

The muddy road is slippery and I almost fall,

The car mocks my madness!

Nonsense 263

— Peng Nian

The success of a difficult undertaking is built on the foundation of a fearless spirit.

Struggle is the key to being a final victor. Inventor Edison and explorer Amundsen are all successful strugglers. Learning and seeking knowledge is like entering the mountains to collect medicine. Without going through deep mountain ravines and rugged roads, there will be no good results.

Hanging plaques with artistic light in dance halls is like writing "clean and hygienic" in the toilet.

Human desires are endless.

A person must first prepare and then do.

How can we move forward? Passive. Discouraged. The road to success. Sure.

If you do it first and then prepare, you'll mess it up.

It's better not to do things that have no results. You must think before you act, so you don't make mistakes.

Patience is a sign of weakness, so patient people lack perseverance.

The Chinese have ended up in this state today because their family concept is too deep.

It is useless to shout slogans and write slogans. Actual work depends entirely on hands and feet.

Relying on others means losing your independence. To maintain your independence, you must ultimately rely on yourself!

People who love luxury and extravagance will inevitably fall, because they will not have the opportunity to reflect.

People say that movies are the birthplace of love. I say that movies are the machine for cultivating knowledge.

Almost all of the world's great people have struggled out of difficult circumstances.

Although homespun cloth is rough, it is very great, because it can restore rights and resist foreign goods, and it can drive away modern girls and approach the working class.

Foolish people can often do incredible things, because they only know how to do and don't know how to think.

Turning in Papers at Five O'Clock, No. 1 264

After eating lunch, it was almost two o'clock in the morning light, and the class bell rang three times. I, who was playing ping-pong in the game room, heard the class bell and quickly put down my paddle and rushed to the classroom.

When I arrived in the classroom, was I the last one? Just as I sat down, Professor C, with his neatly trimmed mustache and air of a "wooden clogs"派, seemed to be following in my footsteps, standing on the podium.

Professor C adjusted himself, then opened his only treasured leather bag, took out more than fifty test papers, and asked Yang X, the leader of the 善武派, to distribute them. He gave a few words in a sermon-like manner, left the podium, and, with his eyes like car headlights, began his rounds as inspector.

"That annoying Chinese language class, I haven't come up with a single sentence yet. I'm afraid it'll be hard to hand in the paper today?" said Chen, nicknamed "Dancing Doctor," and Li, "King of the Bulletin Board."

"Look! Isn't my paper the same as yours? This kind of sly先生 didn't tell us in advance, so we didn't have time to prepare."

"There are only fifteen minutes left! Hurry up and do it. The sooner you hand in the paper, the more points you'll get." Professor C heard them talking and deliberately walked closer to them, saying this to them.

"I can't hand in the paper today. I'll hand it in to you tomorrow. I'm going to fail this semester anyway," said "Dancing Doctor" Chen with a hint of affected pride.

Miss Fan, known for her 校花名, also said to Professor C:

"Professor, today's difficult questions really make it difficult for us to hand in the paper. Let's just wait until tomorrow to hand it in."

"How can that be! The dean has already told me that this exam should be especially strict. If you don't hand in the paper today, won't I have to listen to his complaints?"

"Then, can we hand in a blank paper?"

"Well, you still have to write a few sentences so I can give an account of it," Professor C said, then walked back to the podium.

"Ding, ding, ding!" We heard the end-of-class bell ring, as if escaping from a cage. Everyone walked up to Professor C and asked in unison:

"Hand in the papers at five o'clock."

Professor C had no choice but to slip outside with his leather bag.

Store Clerk Correspondence

How to Reform the Social System? 265

Editor:

Since the publication of my humble work "How to Avenge an Old Friend," I have received your sympathy and guidance. I am also grateful to Mr. 湼 and Mr. Xiong for proposing solutions to the unfortunate encounter of my old friend, Mr. Pan. The plight of my old friend Pan has aroused so much sympathy, which I did not expect!

The dead are gone! The living are unbearable! We should further consider the plight of the exploited, such as Pan, who are still living. As Mr. 湼 said: "It is no longer limited to the problem of individuals, but should be extended to how to reform the social system." I feel that before the entire society is reformed, all individual problems cannot be addressed. We cannot simply curse society, nor should we sit and wait for others to reform society and then let us enjoy the fruits. Every member of society has the mission of transforming society.

However, the question of "how to reform society" cannot be solved by the intellect of one person alone. It must be discussed and studied by the masses before a satisfactory conclusion can be reached. Due to space limitations, I can only outline my views for readers to study and discuss, and I ask the editor to provide guidance.

(1) The Changes in Chinese Society After the Opium War...丨 Before the Opium War, China was a self-sufficient feudal society. Closed off from the world, it could be called a "small well-off." After the Opium War, capitalist countries, after using cannons to invade, continued to invade with a flood of commodities, destroying all the old systems of the rural economy. Whether in economics, politics, ideology, or class relations, dramatic changes occurred. Moreover, because of the impact of imperialist aggression, it not only could not extricate itself but even became a quasi-colonial state.

(2) The Two Major Crises of China's Social Economy: (A) The Abnormal Development of Cities, 丨 Years of banditry, floods, droughts, and foreign agricultural products have accelerated the bankruptcy of rural areas, driving people to concentrate in cities, forming an abnormal development of cities; (B) All major industries, such as railways, shipping, banking, and mining, are in the hands of foreigners; and there is an excess of imports of about one hundred million yuan each year, leading to the danger of economic bankruptcy.

(3) Political Crisis 丨 Imperialist powers, in order to solve their own problems, have had to desperately seize China's rights and interests. The recent Northeast Incident is one example. (4) China's Way Out 丨 To seek a way out for China, it is necessary to remedy the above-mentioned economic and political crises. It is necessary to actively oppose imperialism, get rid of the shackles of imperialism, and expel imperialist forces in China (all economic and political forces). Then China can be unified, and national capital can develop. The first step in anti-imperialism, of course, is to resist Japan and gather the strength of the entire nation to implement resistance against Japan! In short, China cannot get rid of the shackles of imperialism, and the social system cannot be reformed.

This is our vital issue. We hope that readers will enthusiastically participate in the discussion, and we ask the editor to provide guidance. Respectfully, Gu Zhongjie.

January 10 X X X X

Editor's Note: Mr. Gu's letter speaks eloquently about the reasons for China's social ills. The proposed improvement methods are not without merit. However, we believe that the issue of "transforming society" is very broad and complex, with thousands of strands, and cannot be solved with a few words. The far-sighted Premier spent forty or fifty years of research and personally drafted the Three Principles of the People, inventing this all-encompassing, all-inclusive doctrine for saving the country.

In terms of getting rid of the shackles of imperialists, there is nationalism.

In terms of stabilizing society and eliminating man-made disasters, there is democracy.

In terms of stabilizing the economy, developing capital, and revitalizing rural areas, there is the Principle of People's Livelihood. Great are the Three Principles of the People! Those who have the responsibility to improve society, deeply understand them and strive to implement them!

Short Story

Temptation 267

— Translated by Gao Zhixiang, written by E.V. Lucas

"Temptation" is a topic that cannot be discussed frankly in front of acquaintances and strangers alike. However, from this very vague conversation, we can also glean quite a bit of interesting humor.

"My greatest temptation," said a beautiful woman, "was discovered last winter, when I was staying at a not-very-satisfactory hotel by the sea in 立拂來. I was very surprised why I spent so much time there. It turned out I came to get away from the freezing weather, you understand the meaning of that, right?"

Everyone seemed to understand.

"After I had been there for a few days, one evening, some friends from the nearby village invited me to dinner. I happily put on a few fashionable outfits I had bought when I passed through Paris, anticipating getting a lot of compliments then. But, I had to wear my rings, and all the pleasant fantasies vanished. I had a few distinctive rings, so I instructed the maid—she was newly hired—to bring me those rings."

"She took out a few and placed them on the table."

"'No,' I said, 'not those, I want the ones with the emeralds and rubies.'"

"'They're all here,' she said."

"'All here!' I shouted, 'What do you mean? Are the emerald and ruby ones not there? What about the diamond earrings?'"

There was no trace of those things!

I fainted. I thought, this seems to be the fate in this world. Everyone will inevitably encounter a theft sooner or later, but I had never encountered it before.

"Luckily, they were already insured, but I really liked them, so I was very annoyed."

"I and the maid repeatedly, over and over again, checked the jewelry box, searching all possible places, or perhaps possible places. Then I went to report it to the hotel manager."

"He was very polite. He questioned me, but he absolutely didn't believe that such a theft could happen in his place. He asked me if I really brought them—because women are often forgetful."

"'Yes, I definitely brought them.'"

"'Don't you have any suspicions?' he said, glancing at the maid."

"'I believe that the thief must be an outsider.'"

"'But according to our hotel regulations, customers must hand over their valuables to the cashier for safekeeping. But even so, I will do my best to help. If you can give me a detailed list of the lost items, I will report it to the police.'"

"Therefore, I gave a very detailed description of the stolen rings, and then, very troubled and disappointed, I went to the banquet."

"The next day, I saw many policemen constantly coming. The poor maid was interrogated again and again. I felt that every servant there resented me, because of me, they were under suspicion."

"But after questioning, there were no results. The trail of the theft was never found. I hurried back to London, reported it to the insurance company, and entrusted everything to them."

"When many visitors came to inquire, I said that the most grateful people in the world, besides the police—who often return our lost umbrellas to us—are the insurance company employees, because I had already received a check to compensate for the rings, and that was the end of the matter."

Her words stopped.

"'But where is the temptation?' several people in the room asked."

"'I'll continue,' she said, 'The check was mailed in the afternoon. The next day, I went to the bank to deposit it and also to check the safe deposit box stored in the bank.'"

The beautiful lady's words stopped again.

"'What happened?' many people asked."

"'Well,' she said, 'the bank clerk handed me the safe deposit box in the reception room. I opened it—'"

"And the first thing I found was one of the lost rings. The rest were also inside."

"'Ah!' someone in the room shouted."

"'Yes, those things were all stored in the box. Before I went to 立拂來, I had put them away very carefully. But, it was only then that I suddenly remembered. People are often fooled by memory. It's really mysterious. Memory often fails people.'"

"'Now you understand the "temptation," right?' she said, 'On the way home, the "temptation" surrounded me. No one but me knew the truth about the rings. Even the insurance company would never find out. If I were dishonest, I could have the rings and still get a sum of compensation.'" She stopped speaking again.

"'Really!' someone in the room said, and there was silence for a long time.

In every gathering, whether large or small, there is bound to be such a fool who, when everyone understands and is silent, still sincerely asks without thinking, "What did you do?"

Movie Special

Laughable Actions in Art Knowledge Slapstick Films 268

— Chi Zhao

For a film to be considered a slapstick comedy, besides the funny dialogue in the sound era, there are also the laughable actions. Based on my personal observation, the actions that are meant to be funny in many slapstick films can be summarized into the following types:

(1) Playing Dumb: Dumb people are funny, so actors in slapstick films often deliberately act stupidly to make the audience laugh. For example, a comedic character goes to play the piano, but the piano and the chair are too far apart. A normal person would just pull the light chair over, but he has to use all his strength to move the heavy piano closer to the chair. You think, wouldn't this kind of action cause the self-proclaimed intelligent viewers to burst into laughter?

(2) Faking: Faking is also a material that makes people laugh. In slapstick films, a fake action is like a comedic character scaring away a group of robbers with a pistol in his pocket. But, after the group of robbers leaves, he takes the pistol out of his pocket, peels off the skin leisurely and carelessly, revealing the snow-white flesh and chewing it in his mouth. It turns out his pistol is a banana. At that time, the audience will always smile knowingly!

(3) Opposite: Opposite can also be said to be incongruous. When a tall person and a short person stand together, you will laugh at their incongruity. When a big fat person and a thin person bump into each other, you will also laugh at their incongruity. When one person is furious and the other is slow and methodical, you will always find it ridiculous. For example, in the film "葛洛克," when 葛洛克 comes to the stage carrying a large suitcase, he takes out the smallest violin from that large suitcase without any surprise. The audience with keen senses can't help but laugh.

(4) Mistake: It is really funny when someone makes a big mistake while doing something. If you see someone eating a banana without peeling it and eating it with the peel, you will always spread that person as a joke. For example, in the film "Old Soldier," the thin Laurel wants to cut out the advertisement for fertilizer powder in the newspaper. He puts the newspaper on a leather chair and uses a knife to cut the advertisement out. The advertisement is cut out, but he also cuts out a piece of the leather surface of the chair the size of the advertisement. When the audience sees this kind of mistaken action, they will naturally burst into laughter.

The above four types of laughable actions are just what I have observed personally. In addition to these four types, there are certainly many others in slapstick films. However, these four types are commonly seen, and for each of the four types, I have only given one example to generalize the others. Omissions are unavoidable.

Overseas Anecdotes

Dietrich's Problems 269

— Yi Hua

Hollywood is now very eagerly discussing Marlene Dietrich's problems. Because her contract with Paramount Pictures will expire in February of this month. Will she still renew it? Will she accept directors other than Von Sternberg? What is her relationship with Sivil? There are many questions.

She hadn't expressed any opinion for a long time, but recently she cordially received news reporters! Announcing her future whereabouts.

She said that her contract with Von Sternberg expired after the recent completion of a film. She said very firmly that she would no longer stay in Hollywood, but would prepare to sing in Paris, Berlin, and London.

She said that her appearance on the screen was not for money. Money was not a big deal to her. She joined Paramount entirely at the urging of Von Sternberg. So maybe she will still accept his persuasion and stay in Hollywood, but she only wants to be directed by Sternberg alone.

Regarding the various rumors about her and Sivil, she said: "Outsiders may have forgotten that I am a married woman. My husband and I have never considered divorce. He is still having a happy Christmas."

Marlene has been in Hollywood for three and a half years, completing a total of five films. However, with just these five films, she has already occupied an important position in Hollywood.

In short, the mysterious Dietrich is just like Garbo's second!

Shortcomings in the Chinese Film Industry 270

— Zong Wen

(A) Some actors clearly do not need to be the leading role in a certain play, but they insist on being so, simply because they are ashamed to be inferior to others. By the time the play is filmed and people criticize their shortcomings, it is already too late!

(B) The shortcomings of companies mutually denigrating each other. If a company has a good actor, they are often poached by another company. As a result, the originally good partnership cannot last forever, and the film is greatly diminished!

(C) There are often disagreements in companies, so that if a company has a good director, but the actors have incompatible personalities, the result will certainly not be a good film.

(D) Lack of the spirit of international promotion.

Loretta Young's "Premature Maturity" 271

— Shi Chun

Those who have seen "The Gold Diggers" should be familiar with Loretta Young's skills. Although she is a supporting actress, she adds a lot of brilliance to the film. She is only nineteen years old this year, but she has already been married and divorced, and has been a housewife, managing household affairs and property very shrewdly.

Loretta has been sophisticated since she was a child. At the age of sixteen, she already had a lover. When her parents tried to restrain her slightly, she left home and lived with her lover. At the age of eighteen, she had a falling out with her good lover and divorced. After the divorce, because she was lonely, she lived with her mother and sisters.

Loretta entered the film industry at a young age. She knows the situation in the film industry like the back of her hand. She says that the changes in the film industry are unpredictable, so once she finds a suitable partner and marries him, she is determined to leave the film industry.

Filmmaker Shao Renmei Returns to China 272

— Hui Feng

Shao Renmei, the general manager of the Seastar Company in Singapore, is the younger brother of Shao Zuiweng, the general manager of the Tianyi Film Company. He is very straightforward, capable, and full of courageous and enterprising spirit. In 1927, he went to the South Seas Islands to investigate the film business, and then co-founded the Seastar Company in Singapore with local overseas Chinese, managing Chinese and foreign films. He also founded many cinemas in Singapore, Kuala Lumpur, Penang, Seremban, Ipoh, Yangon, and other places. In the South Seas film industry, Mr. Shao is truly a giant. In 1930, he also went to Japan to study sound films. Last year, when Tianyi Company started filming Movietone sound films, Mr. Shao returned to China to assist in the process, and then returned to the South Seas. It is now reported that Mr. Shao arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 16th, and Shao Zuiweng, Shao Cunren, and others went to the pier to greet him.

— Ye Min

Originally, Ruan Lingyu, Chen Yumei, and Hu Die were known as the representative stars of the three major companies. Since Liming Hui returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong and re-entered the film industry, a new term, "Four Great Diamonds," has been coined. (Referring to Hu, Ruan, Chen, and Li.) However, apart from Chen and Li both belonging to Tianyi, Hu is in Mingxing and Ruan is in Lianhua, so there are very few opportunities for them to gather together. The day before yesterday, Chen Yumei hosted a banquet for the major stars at her home. In addition to Hu, Ruan, and Li all attending, there were also Xu Qinfang, Hu Shan, Tang Xueqing, Fan Xuepeng, Xu Lai, etc. It was truly a gathering of beauties, an unprecedented event. And the "Four Great Diamonds," who rarely gather together, exchanged toasts and drank freely together. The most eloquent person at the table was the little sister Liming Hui. Hu, Ruan, and others were also in particularly good spirits, teasing each other with laughter. The hostess, Chen Yumei, wore light makeup and a dark outfit and did not speak much. Halfway through the banquet, the hostess invited the stars to take a photo together to commemorate the occasion. So they ran to the studio at home and took a group photo. In the front row of the picture (from left to right) are Chen Yumei, Hu Die, Liming Hui, Ruan Lingyu, and Xu Qinfang. In the back row (from left to right) are Hu Shan, Tang Xueqing, Xu Lai, and Fan Xuepeng.

The "Match King" Story (12) 274

— Translated by Xi Meng

Erick looked at Paul's face with eyes like a child admiring his father. He also knew Paul's thoughts, but the Match King's business had grown so large, and the debt was so alarming, that if Paul didn't use his extraordinary talent, the iceberg would be in danger of collapsing.

But a few weeks later, Paul bought a train ticket again to go to 利佛拉 in France. He wanted to send a telegram to invite 慕爾娜 to go with him. Before he finished sending the telegram, Erick ran in. Paul smiled at him, with an indescribable joy in his heart, "This time I'm really going. I won't even tell you where I'm going, so you don't come to 陸慈堡 to find me and bring me back like last time. I'm going to heaven to rest for three weeks."

"Of course, that's as it should be," Erick said with a smile. "But 尼伯格 is outside, he wants to see you. Won't you see him? He wouldn't tell me why he wanted to see you, he just said the matter was extremely important."

"Okay, tell him to come in," Paul thought that nothing in the world could stop him now. He held the train ticket in his pocket, thinking that nothing in the world was impossible.

"Ask him to come in, maybe he can tell me that Japanese matches were found on a German ship in Liverpool!"

尼伯格 was one of Paul's secret detectives, and now he came in. He had a face full of pockmarks, so he brought amazing news, and his face didn't show it at all.

Paul jumped up.

"Nothing of the sort," Paul's eyes widened. He told Erick to leave.

"It's absolutely true," 尼伯格 stated solemnly. His name is 克禮斯欽霍勃. The self-lighting invention that can be struck, lit, blown out, and then struck and lit again. That is a perpetual match. This is of great importance to our future. But that man trusts me very much, and I can find a way to get his detailed explanation.

"I'll go with you," Paul said suddenly. 慕爾娜 and the train ticket in his pocket were all thrown to Java.

This matter went very smoothly. He got the inventor's instructions without any effort. He knew its content tomorrow, besides the old inventor, there was no third person in the world. The old man also believed that the Match King could definitely help him, so he frankly handed the instructions to Paul 克魯爾.

Paul 克魯爾 returned to the office and made a phone call.

At Paul, the phone call was 保, creating endless future troubles; but for the old inventor, it was a permanent confinement in a lunatic asylum, his mad roar, it was　　's surface　!
